Deny popup request\r\n2. Allow popup request\r\n3. Open popup request in a background tab\r\n4. Redirect current page to popup URL source\r\n\r\nSupported blocking methods:\r\n1. window.open\r\n2. a->target=_blank\r\n\r\nFor bug reports please go to:\r\nhttps://github.com/schomery/popup-blocker/issues\r\n\r\nFor FAQs please go to:\r\nhttp://add0n.com/popup-blocker.html\r\n\r\nFor testing your current popup blocker effectiveness go to:\r\nhttp://tools.add0n.com/popup-blocker.html\r\n\r\n---\r\nYou can now translate Popup Blocker (strict) into your language; https://www.transifex.com/github-7/popup-blocker-strict/\r\n---\r\n\r\nChange Log:\r\nversion 0.2.8:\r\n1. If mouse is hovered over the popup notification, the counter stops counting so that user can review the popup request\r\n2.
